	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　魅音は元の、いつもの笑顔に戻ると、俺の手を強く引き、石段を駆け下りていった…。",
		   NULL, "Mion torna al sorriso che aveva un attimo fa, per poi continuare a tirarmi la mano e a scendere giù per le scale...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
//■８日目幕間
//if %kaisou_mode = 1 goto *kaisou_mode
//mov ?Tip[31],TIPS_NEW : mov ?GET_TIPS_BUF[%NEW_TIPS],TIPS_031 :mov %TIPS_031,2:inc %NEW_TIPS
//mov ?Tip[32],TIPS_NEW : mov ?GET_TIPS_BUF[%NEW_TIPS],TIPS_032 :mov %TIPS_032,2:inc %NEW_TIPS
//mov ?Tip[33],TIPS_NEW : mov ?GET_TIPS_BUF[%NEW_TIPS],TIPS_033 :mov %TIPS_033,2:inc %NEW_TIPS
//mov %CAMP_MUGIC,0
//gosub *Sub_Camp_Mode

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
//	DrawBustshot( 5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
//	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 3000 );

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/wata008", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 5000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
	DrawSceneWithMask("black", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
